| 2:20:45| Sir, if I could, members of the board.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8445)|
| 2:20:47| You have to distinguish between those boards under which you have appointed power| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8447)|
| 2:20:51| under the charter or the code and those that are creatures of statute.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8451)|
| 2:20:55| Under your code, you have the authority by resolution to remove| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8455)|
| 2:20:58| and discharge anyone you appoint.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8458)|
| 2:21:01| However, if you're dealing with a board where in the state has preemptive| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8461)|
| 2:21:05| such as a BZA, you can remove someone for cause upon written charges| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8465)|
| 2:21:11| and after a public hearing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8471)|
| 2:21:13| So the bottom line is in terms of it being retroactive or ex post facto,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8473)|
| 2:21:17| the bottom line is if it is a state appointed board like BZA,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8477)|
| 2:21:21| which empowers you to create a BZA,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8481)|
| 2:21:23| you could at any time inform the member in question in writing that they're about to be discharged,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8483)|
| 2:21:30| then you give them a public hearing, and then if the board votes, they're gone.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8490)|
| 2:21:33| If it's anybody else, you do a resolution, they're gone.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8493)|
| 2:21:36| So regardless of what you pass today,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8496)|
| 2:21:38| you already have the authority to remove people from your appointed boards.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom100222part1?start=8498)|
